\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    
    
    \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
    % Nicer default font (+ math font) than Computer Modern for most use cases
    \usepackage{mathpazo}

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % We will generate all images so they have a width \maxwidth. This means
    % that they will get their normal width if they fit onto the page, but
    % are scaled down if they would overflow the margins.
    \makeatletter
    \def\maxwidth{\ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth\linewidth
    \else\Gin@nat@width\fi}
    \makeatother
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Set max figure width to be 80% of text width, for now hardcoded.
    \renewcommand{\includegraphics}[1]{\Oldincludegraphics[width=.8\maxwidth]{#1}}
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionLabelFormat{nolabel}{}
    \captionsetup{labelformat=nolabel}

    \usepackage{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size 
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro
    \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs} % Extended unicode (utf-8) support
    \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc} % Allow utf-8 characters in the tex document
    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics 
                         % to support a larger range 
    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines

    \definecolor{urlcolor}{rgb}{0,.145,.698}

    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}9}]:} \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{cooccurrence\PYZus{}matrix}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{list\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{distance}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{sentances}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZsq{}\PYZsq{}\PYZsq{}}
        \PY{l+s+sd}{    Returns co\PYZhy{}occurrence matrix of words with in a distance of occurrrence}
        \PY{l+s+sd}{    input:}
        \PY{l+s+sd}{        list\PYZus{}words: list of words to get the co\PYZhy{}occurrance matrix in order}
        \PY{l+s+sd}{        distance: distance between words}
        \PY{l+s+sd}{        sentances: documets to check ( a list )}
        \PY{l+s+sd}{    output:}
        \PY{l+s+sd}{        co\PYZhy{}occurance matrix in te order of list\PYZus{}words order}
        \PY{l+s+sd}{    \PYZsq{}\PYZsq{}\PYZsq{}}
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}length of matrix needed}
            \PY{n}{l} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{list\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}creating a zero matrix }
            \PY{n}{com} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{zeros}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{l}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{l}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}creating word and index dict}
            \PY{n}{dict\PYZus{}idx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{v}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{i} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{v} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{enumerate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{list\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
            \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{sentence} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{sentances}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{n}{sentence}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{sentence}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{n}{tokens}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sentence}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{pos}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{token} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{enumerate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{tokens}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}if  eord is in required words}
                    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{token} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{list\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{:}
                        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}start index to check any other word occure or not}
                        \PY{n}{start}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n+nb}{max}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{pos}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{distance}\PY{p}{)}
                        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}end index}
                        \PY{n}{end}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n+nb}{min}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{tokens}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{pos}\PY{o}{+}\PY{n}{distance}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
                        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{pos2} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{start}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{end}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}if same position }
                            \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{pos2}\PY{o}{==}\PY{n}{pos}\PY{p}{:} 
                                \PY{k}{continue}
                            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} if same word}
                            \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{token} \PY{o}{==} \PY{n}{tokens}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{pos2}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{:}
                                \PY{k}{continue}
                            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}if word found is in required words}
                            \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{tokens}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{pos2}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{list\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{:}
                                \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}index of word parent}
                                \PY{n}{row} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{dict\PYZus{}idx}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{token}\PY{p}{]}
                                \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}index of occurance word}
                                \PY{n}{col} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{dict\PYZus{}idx}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{tokens}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{pos2}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}
                                \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}adding value to that index}
                                \PY{n}{com}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{com}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
            \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{com}
\end{Verbatim}

    We can obsever some similar words in clusters, like\\

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}10}]:} \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{top\PYZus{}similar\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{v}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{Wordvectors}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{list\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{    Gives output angles between one vector(v1) and all other vectors as matrix(v2)}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{    input:}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{        v  shape (d,1)}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{        Wordvectors shape (m,d)}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{        n \PYZhy{} no of similarities needed}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{        list\PYZus{}words \PYZhy{} list of all words in Wordvectors in same order}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{    output:}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{        list of n words which are similar}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{    \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
             \PY{n}{v1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{v}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n}{v1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{v1}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n}{v2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Wordvectors}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}dot product}
             \PY{n}{nr} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dot}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{v2}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{v1}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}vector lengths 2\PYZhy{}norm}
             \PY{n}{dr} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{linalg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{norm}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{v1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{*}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{linalg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{norm}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{v2}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{axis}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} angle i.e cosine inverse and domine for cosine inverse is }
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} [\PYZhy{}1,1] so clipping to [\PYZhy{}1,1] and claculating angle}
             \PY{n}{ang} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{arccos}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{clip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{nr}\PY{o}{/}\PY{n}{dr}\PY{p}{,}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n}{ang} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{ang}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{ravel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}sorting and getting index of top n }
             \PY{n}{ang\PYZus{}10} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{argsort}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{ang}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{n}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
             \PY{n}{ang\PYZus{}n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{delete}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{ang\PYZus{}10}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n}{dict\PYZus{}tfidf} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{v} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{v} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{enumerate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{list\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
             \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{dict\PYZus{}tfidf}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{ang\PYZus{}n}\PY{p}{]}
\end{Verbatim}
